## ğŸ¨ DESIGN SYSTEM RECAP

### Color Palette

```
Primary (Indigo):
  50:  #EEF2FF
  500: #6366F1  â† Main brand
  700: #4338CA

Success (Green):
  500: #10B981

Warning (Amber):
  500: #F59E0B

Danger (Red):
  500: #EF4444

Neutral (Gray):
  50:  #F9FAFB  â† Backgrounds
  100: #F3F4F6
  200: #E5E7EB  â† Borders
  500: #6B7280  â† Text secondary
  900: #111827  â† Text primary
```

### Typography Scale

```
Hero:     4xl (2.25rem)  â†’ Homepage hero
H1:       3xl (1.875rem) â†’ Page titles
H2:       2xl (1.5rem)   â†’ Section titles
H3:       xl  (1.25rem)  â†’ Sub-sections
Body:     base (1rem)    â†’ Default text
Small:    sm  (0.875rem) â†’ Secondary text
Tiny:     xs  (0.75rem)  â†’ Labels, hints
```

### Spacing Scale

```
xs:  4px   â†’ Icon spacing
sm:  8px   â†’ Tight spacing
md:  16px  â†’ Default spacing
lg:  24px  â†’ Section spacing
xl:  32px  â†’ Large gaps
2xl: 48px  â†’ Major sections
```

### Component States

```
Default:  Normal state
Hover:    Subtle bg change + cursor pointer
Active:   Pressed state
Focus:    Blue ring (accessibility)
Disabled: Opacity 50%, cursor not-allowed
Loading:  Spinner + disabled state
Error:    Red border + error message
Success:  Green border + checkmark
```
